This is the result of a large sweep of convolution parameters.
All images and filters are square. Tiles are square except for the edge tiles potentially.
Weights are chosen to avoid overflow (this is poor-man's training equivalent).

* Image size (h31 is an image 31*31)
* Filter size (r4 is a filter 4*4)
* Stride (s3 is stride of 3 in both X and Y dimension)
* Number of input channels, IFMAPs. (c64 is 64 input channels)
* Number of output channels,OFMAPs. (m3 is 3 output channels)

Jan 23, 2018:
Many tests fail due to a bug where for tiles smaller than images
some of filter weights multiply zero image pixels. The simulator
does not accept zero pixels, so I am changing code to not issue any
instruction for this case.
